add_namespace = csa

### Constitution Events ###

###Social Patriots
country_event = { # Socialist Constitution - Property Debate
	id = csa.1000
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event csa.1000"}
	title = csa.1000.t
	desc = csa.1000.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_congress

	is_triggered_only = yes

	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = { #The Laborists win out
		name = csa.1000.a	
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_democrat
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = totalist
			popularity = 0.02
		}
		hidden_effect = {
		country_event = {
			id = csa.1001
			days = 7
			}
			set_country_flag = {
			flag = CSA_afl
			value = 1
			}
			set_country_flag = {
			flag = CSA_browder
			value = 1
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # The Nationalists win out
		name = csa.1000.b
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = radical_socialist
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = totalist
			popularity = 0.03
		}
		hidden_effect = {
		country_event = {
			id = csa.1001
			days = 7
			}
			set_country_flag = {
			flag = CSA_nationalists
			value = 1
			}
			set_country_flag = {
			flag = CSA_burnham
			value = 1
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Socialist Constitution - Social Radicalism
	id = csa.1001
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event csa.1001"}
	title = csa.1001.t
	desc = csa.1001.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_congress

	is_triggered_only = yes

	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = { #The Laborists win out
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CSA_post_civil_war
						option = CSA_POST_CIVIL_WAR_BURNHAM
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CSA_post_civil_war
						option = CSA_POST_CIVIL_WAR_LOVESTONE
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CSA_post_civil_war
						option = CSA_POST_CIVIL_WAR_LOVESTONE
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CSA_post_civil_war
						option = CSA_POST_CIVIL_WAR_NATIONALIST
					}
				}
			}
		}
		name = csa.1001.a
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_democrat
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = totalist
			popularity = 0.03
		}	
		hidden_effect = {
		country_event = {
			id = csa.1002
			days = 7
			}
			modify_country_flag = {
			flag = CSA_afl
			value = 1
				}
			modify_country_flag = {
			flag = CSA_burnham
			value = 1
				}
			}
		}
	option = { # The Nationalists win out
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CSA_post_civil_war
						option = CSA_POST_CIVIL_WAR_BROWDER
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CSA_post_civil_war
						option = CSA_POST_CIVIL_WAR_FEDERALIST
					}
				}
			}
		}
		name = csa.1001.b
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = radical_socialist
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = totalist
			popularity = 0.02
		}
		hidden_effect = {
		country_event = {
			id = csa.1002
			days = 7
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			modify_country_flag = {
			flag = CSA_nationalists
			value = 1
			}
			modify_country_flag = {
			flag = CSA_browder
			value = 1
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Socialist Constitution - Voting Rights
	id = csa.1002

			factor = 25

country_event = { # Socialist Election Arrives
	id = csa.1003
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event csa.1003"}
	title = csa.1003.t
	desc = csa.1003.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_congress

	is_triggered_only = yes

	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = { #The Independence League
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CSA_post_civil_war
						option = CSA_POST_CIVIL_WAR_BURNHAM
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CSA_post_civil_war
						option = CSA_POST_CIVIL_WAR_LOVESTONE
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CSA_post_civil_war
						option = CSA_POST_CIVIL_WAR_BROWDER
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CSA_post_civil_war
						option = CSA_POST_CIVIL_WAR_FEDERALIST
					}
				}
			}
		}
		name = csa.1003.a
		trigger = {
		OR = {
		NOT = {
		has_country_flag = CSA_Laborite_Plan
		}
		has_country_flag = {
			flag = CSA_nationalists
			value > 2
			}
		}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
		country_event = {
		id = csa.901
		days = 6
		}
		country_event = {
		id = csa.330
		days = 5
		}
		set_country_flag = CSA_Nationalist_Victory
		}
		set_country_flag = CSA_constitutional_convention_done
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = radical_socialist
			election_frequency = 48
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
	}
	option = { # The AFL
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CSA_post_civil_war
						option = CSA_POST_CIVIL_WAR_BURNHAM
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CSA_post_civil_war
						option = CSA_POST_CIVIL_WAR_LOVESTONE
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CSA_post_civil_war
						option = CSA_POST_CIVIL_WAR_NATIONALIST
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CSA_post_civil_war
						option = CSA_POST_CIVIL_WAR_BROWDER
					}
				}
			}
		}
		name = csa.1003.b
		trigger = {
		OR = {
		has_country_flag = CSA_Laborite_Plan
		has_country_flag = {
			flag = CSA_afl
			value > 2
			}
		}
		}
		set_country_flag = CSA_constitutional_convention_done
		hidden_effect = {
		country_event = {
		id = csa.901
		days = 6
		}
		country_event = {
		id = csa.325
		days = 5
		}
		set_country_flag = CSA_AFL_In_Power
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = social_democrat
			election_frequency = 48
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
	}
	option = { # Browder's SPA Centralist Ticket
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CSA_post_civil_war
						option = CSA_POST_CIVIL_WAR_BURNHAM
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CSA_post_civil_war
						option = CSA_POST_CIVIL_WAR_LOVESTONE
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CSA_post_civil_war
						option = CSA_POST_CIVIL_WAR_NATIONALIST
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CSA_post_civil_war
						option = CSA_POST_CIVIL_WAR_FEDERALIST
					}
				}
			}
		}
		name = csa.1003.c
		trigger = {
		has_country_flag = {
			flag = CSA_browder
			value > 2
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = CSA_constitutional_convention_done
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
			id = csa.901
			days = 6
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					BBR = {
						has_country_leader = { ruling_only = yes name = "Harry Haywood"}
					}
				}
				BBR = {
					country_event = {
						id = bbr.28
						days = 35
					}
				}
			}
			add_ideas = CSA_Ernest_Hemingway_for_tot
			add_ideas = CSA_Gus_Hall_eco_tot
			add_ideas = CSA_Steve_Nelson_sec_tot
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Earl Browder"
				desc = "POLITICS_EARL_BROWDER_DESC"
				picture = "Portrait_CSA_Earl_Bowder.png"
				expire = "1965.1.1"
				ideology = totalist_subtype
				traits = { the_director }
			}
			country_event = {
				id = csa.71
				days = 365
			}
			country_event = {
				id = csa.72
				days = 380
			}
			country_event = {
				id = csa.74
				days = 430
			}
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = totalist
			election_frequency = 48
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = totalist
			long_name = CSA_totalist_syndicalism_party_long
			name = CSA_totalist_syndicalism_party
		}
		hidden_effect = {
		set_country_flag = CSA_Nationalists_in_power
		}
	}
	option = { # The American Worker's Party
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CSA_post_civil_war
						option = CSA_POST_CIVIL_WAR_BROWDER
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CSA_post_civil_war
						option = CSA_POST_CIVIL_WAR_NATIONALIST
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CSA_post_civil_war
						option = CSA_POST_CIVIL_WAR_FEDERALIST
					}
				}
			}
		}
		name = csa.1003.e
		trigger = {
		has_country_flag = {
			flag = CSA_burnham
			value > 2
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
		country_event = {
		id = csa.901
		days = 6
		}
		set_country_flag = CSA_burnham_is_leader
		set_country_flag = CSA_constitutional_convention_done
			add_ideas = CSA_Joseph_Zack_Kornfeder_for_tot
			add_ideas = CSA_Frederick_L_Ackerman_eco_tot
			add_ideas = CSA_Lawrence_Dennis_sec_tot 
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "James Burnham"
				desc = "POLITICS_JAMES_BURNHAM_DESC"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/CSA/Portrait_CSA_burnham.png"
				expire = "1965.1.1"
				ideology = technocratic_socialism_subtype
				traits = { managerialist }
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = { id = csa.165 days = 8 }
				country_event = { id = csa.273 months = 2 }
			}
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = totalist
			election_frequency = 48
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = totalist
			long_name = CSA_totalist_syndicalism_party_long
			name = CSA_totalist_syndicalism_party
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				BBR = {
					has_country_leader = { ruling_only = yes name = "Harry Haywood"}
				}
			}
			BBR = {
				country_event = {
					id = bbr.28
					days = 35
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Constitutional Convention begins
	id = csa.1
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event csa.1"}
	title = csa.1.t
	desc = csa.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_congress

    fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = csa.1.a
		hidden_effect = {
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "CSA Central Committee"
				desc = "POLITICS_CSA_CENTRAL_COMITTEE_DESC"
				picture = "Portrait_CSA_committee.png"
				expire = "1965.1.1"
				ideology = radical_socialist_subtype
				traits = {
					our_right_to_survive
				}
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "CSA Central Committee"
				desc = "POLITICS_CSA_CENTRAL_COMITTEE_DESC"
				picture = "Portrait_CSA_committee.png"
				expire = "1965.1.1"
				ideology = syndicalist_subtype
				traits = {
					our_right_to_survive
				}
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "CSA Central Committee"
				desc = "POLITICS_CSA_CENTRAL_COMITTEE_DESC"
				picture = "Portrait_CSA_committee.png"
				expire = "1965.1.1"
				ideology = totalist_subtype
				traits = {
					our_right_to_survive

			}

				flag = CSA_radicals
				value = 0
			}
			country_event = {
				id = csa.2
				days = 7
			}
		}
	}
}

			ideology = syndicalist

				days = 1
			}
		}
	}

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1

				factor = 0

		name = csa.10.a

			id = csa.11
			days = 3
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = CSA_syndicalism
				}
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = totalist

					name = CSA_totalist_syndicalism_party
				}
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = syndicalist
					long_name = CSA_syndicalist_party_syndicalism_long
					name = CSA_syndicalist_syndicalism_party
				}
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = radical_socialist
					long_name = CSA_radical_socialist_syndicalism_party_long
					name = CSA_radical_socialist_syndicalism_party
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = CSA_socialist
				}
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = totalist
					long_name = CSA_totalist_federalist_party_long
					name = CSA_totalist_federalist_party
				}
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = syndicalist
					long_name = CSA_syndicalist_federalist_party_long
					name = CSA_syndicalist_federalist_party
				}
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = radical_socialist
					long_name = CSA_radical_socialist_federalist_party_long
					name = CSA_radical_socialist_federalist_party
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = CSA_capital_chicago
			}
			set_capital = 395
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = CSA_capital_washington
			}
			set_capital = 361
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = CSA_capital_philly
			}
			set_capital = 360
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = CSA_capital_nyc
			}
			set_capital = 358
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # 1952 Election
	id = csa.36
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event csa.36"}
	title = csa.36.t
	desc = csa.36.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_election_vote

	trigger = {
		tag = CSA
		has_country_flag = CSA_constitutional_convention_done
		has_country_flag = CSA_had_1940_election
		has_country_flag = CSA_had_1944_election
		has_country_flag = CSA_had_1948_election
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = CSA_had_1952_election
		}
		OR = {
			has_government = radical_socialist
			has_government = syndicalist
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = { # Eugene Dennis
				limit = { has_country_flag = CSA_1952_iww_primary_dennis }
				kill_ideology_leader = syndicalist
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Eugene Dennis"
					desc = "POLITICS_EUGENE_DENNIS_DESC"
					picture = "Portrait_CSA_Eugene_Dennis.png"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = syndicalist_subtype
					traits = {
						indecisive
					}
				}
			}
			if = { # Henning A. Blomen
				limit = { has_country_flag = CSA_1952_iww_primary_blomen }
				kill_ideology_leader = syndicalist
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Henning A. Blomen"
					desc = "POLITICS_HENNING_BLOMEN_DESC"
					picture = "Portrait_CSA_Henning_A_Blomen.png"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = syndicalist_subtype
					traits = {
						captain_of_industry
					}
				}
			}
			if = { # John Bernard
				limit = { has_country_flag = CSA_1952_iww_primary_bernard }
				kill_ideology_leader = syndicalist
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "John Bernard"
					desc = "POLITICS_JOHN_BERNARD_DESC"
					picture = "Portrait_CSA_John_Bernard.png"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = syndicalist_subtype
					traits = {
						warmonger
					}
				}
			}
			if = { # Oakley C. Johnson
				limit = { has_country_flag = CSA_1952_cio_primary_johnson }
				kill_ideology_leader = radical_socialist
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Oakley C. Johnson"
					desc = "POLITICS_OAKLEY_JOHNSON_DESC"
					picture = "Portrait_CSA_Oakley_C_Johnson.png"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = radical_socialist_subtype
					traits = {
						editor
					}
				}
			}
			if = { # Bayard Rustin
				limit = { has_country_flag = CSA_1952_cio_primary_rustin }
				kill_ideology_leader = radical_socialist
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Bayard Rustin"
					desc = "POLITICS_BAYARD_RUSTIN_DESC"
					picture = "Portrait_CSA_Bayard_Rustin.png"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = radical_socialist_subtype
					traits = {
						great_survivor
					}
				}
			}
			if = { # Darlington Hoopes
				limit = { has_country_flag = CSA_1952_cio_primary_hoopes }
				kill_ideology_leader = radical_socialist
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Darlington Hoopes"
					desc = "POLITICS_DARLINGTON_HOOPES_DESC"
					picture = "Portrait_CSA_Darlington_Hoopes.png"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = radical_socialist_subtype
					traits = {
						captain_of_industry
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # IWW
		name = csa.36.a
		set_country_flag = CSA_had_1952_election
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = csa_1952_election_iww
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = syndicalist
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = syndicalist
			election_frequency = 48
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = csa.40
				days = 1
			}
			#no more primaries
		}
	}

country_event = { # The election(totalist)
	id = csa.51
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event csa.51"}
	title = csa.51.t
	desc = csa.51.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_election_vote

	trigger = {
		tag = CSA
		has_country_flag = CSA_constitutional_convention_done
		has_government = totalist
		NOT = { has_completed_focus = CSA_proletariat_commander }
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		modify_country_flag = {
			flag = CSA_totalist_elections
			value = 1
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = csa.51.a
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = {
				flag = CSA_totalist_elections
				value > 0
			}
			has_country_flag = {
				flag = CSA_totalist_elections
				value < 2
			}
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = totalist
			popularity = 0.10
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = totalist
			election_frequency = 48
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = csa.51.b
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = {
				flag = CSA_totalist_elections
				value > 1
			}
			has_country_flag = {
				flag = CSA_totalist_elections
				value < 3
			}
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = totalist
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = totalist
			election_frequency = 48
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = csa.51.c
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = {
				flag = CSA_totalist_elections
				value > 2
			}
			has_country_flag = {
				flag = CSA_totalist_elections
				value < 4
			}
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = totalist
			election_frequency = 48
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = csa.51.e
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = {
				flag = CSA_totalist_elections
				value > 3
			}
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = totalist
			popularity = -0.05
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = totalist
			election_frequency = 48
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
	}
}

		}
	}

					option = CSA_POST_CIVIL_WAR_FOSTER
				}
			}
		}
		add_stability = -0.2

			popularity = -0.25
		}

				id = csa.68
				days = 7
			}
		}

		remove_all_ministers = yes
		create_country_leader = {
			name = "Smedley Butler"
			desc = "POLITICS_SMEDLY_BUTLER_DESC"

			expire = "1965.1.1"
			ideology = radical_socialist_subtype
			traits = { cornered_fox }
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = radical_socialist
			elections_allowed = no
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = csa.67.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
			modifier = {
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = CSA_post_civil_war
					option = CSA_POST_CIVIL_WAR_BUTLER
				}
			}
		}
		add_stability = -0.1
		add_political_power = -250
		remove_unit_leader = 960 #Butler
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = CSA_Smedley_Butler_cos
			}
			remove_ideas = CSA_Smedley_Butler_cos
		}
		set_country_flag = Smedley_Butler_dead
	}
}

		}
	}

country_event = { # Overtures to Mexico
	id = csa.130
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event csa.130"}
	title = csa.130.t
	desc = csa.130.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_diplomacy2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = csa.130.a #Agree
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 90
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				has_opinion = {
					target = FROM
					value < 0
				}
			}
		}
		add_stability = 0.05
		add_political_power = 100
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = FROM
			modifier = USA_american_trade
		}
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = FROM
			modifier = ITA_likes_govt
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_subject = no
				NOT = {
					is_guaranteed_by = FROM
				}
			}
			FROM = {
				give_guarantee = MEX
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					gives_military_access_to = FROM
				}
			}
			give_military_access = FROM
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_mainland_america = yes
				NOT = {
					is_core_of = MEX
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_claimed_by = MEX
				}
				remove_claim_by = MEX
			}
			CSA = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						is_core_of = FROM
						is_claimed_by = FROM
					}
					is_mainland_america = no
					is_core_of = MEX
				}
				MEX = {
					transfer_state = PREV
				}
			}
			country_event = {
				id = csa.131
				hours = 8
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = csa.130.b #Refuse
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					is_subject_of = FROM
					is_in_faction_with = FROM
					has_opinion = {
						target = FROM
						value > 50
					}
				}
			}
		}
		add_stability = -0.05
		add_political_power = -50
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = FROM
			modifier = ITA_dislikes_govt
		}
		FROM = {
			country_event = {
				id = csa.132
				hours = 8
			}
		}
	}
}

						}
					}

			}

				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = CSA_iron_brigades_idea_1
					add_idea = CSA_iron_brigades_idea_reinforced

				hidden_effect = {

	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event csa.212"}
	title = csa.212.t
	desc = csa.212.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_chicago

	fire_only_once = yes
	
	trigger = {
		has_idea = CSA_war_syndicalism_idea
		has_completed_focus = CSA_military_industrial_complex
		OR = {
			has_country_flag = mescaline_use
			date > 1944.08.01
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = csa.212.a
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = CSA_war_syndicalism_idea
			add_idea = CSA_state_of_war_idea
		}
	}
}

		}
	}

		name = csa.2700.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NEE = {
					exists = yes
					is_ai = no
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {

						is_subject_of = ROOT
					}
				}
				end_puppet = NEE
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_in_faction_with = NEE
				}
				NEE = {
					leave_faction = yes
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NEE = {
						exists = yes
						has_war = yes
					}
				}
				NEE = {
					separate_peace_all_wars = yes
				}
			}
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_owned_by = CAN
				OR = {
					state = 357 #Maine
					state = 934 #New Hampshire
					state = 933 #Vermont
					state = 932 #Massachusetts
					state = 935 #Rhode Island
					state = 931 #Connecticut
					state = 796 #Upstate New York
				}
			}
			effect_tooltip = {
				if = {
					limit = { is_claimed_by = CAN }
					remove_claim_by = CAN
				}
				FROM = {
					transfer_state = PREV
				}
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			country_event = {
				id = csa.2701
				days = 1
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # We shall never give into yankee arrogance
		name = csa.2700.b

			factor = 80
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				OR = {

					has_war_with = FRA
					has_war_with = ENG
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_in_faction_with = FROM
				NEE = {
					OR = {
						exists = no
						is_ai = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			country_event = {
				id = csa.2702
				days = 1
			}
		}
	}
}

			name = "Jay Lovestone"
			desc = "POLITICS_JAY_LOVESTONE_DESC"

			}

		ruling_party = totalist

		limit = { has_idea = CSA_proletariat_commander_idea }
		remove_ideas = CSA_proletariat_commander_idea
		}
		else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = CSA_proletariat_commander_idea_2 }
		remove_ideas = CSA_proletariat_commander_idea_2
		}
		add_political_power = -75
		add_stability = -0.1
		add_popularity = { ideology = totalist popularity = -0.03 }
		CSA = {
			country_event = {
				id = csa.516
				days = 6
			}
		}
	}
}
